![夜海无人机艺术字形投影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988124005_fzyiut_G9FShwyboAAhHaO.jpg)

```
[参照画像の特徴：入力画像]
上記の特徴を持つキャラクターの形を、夜空に浮かぶ無数の発光するドローンが形成しているリアルな写真。
場所は夜の海の上空。暗い空に数千個のドローンのLEDライトが点描画のように配置され、鮮やかなネオンカラーでキャラクターを夜空に描いている。
ドローンの光が下の暗い海面に反射して揺らいでいる。

### 8. 适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的多语言人物产品介绍布局提示

**Author**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细、结构化的提示，旨在将角色的参考图像转换为逼真的 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局，包括产品信息、徽标和特写视图。此提示支持生成日语、英语、德语和法语的产品详细信息文本，并需要提供角色的参考图像。

![适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的多语言人物产品介绍布局提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988108612_fjlo36_G9ERMHIb0AIk0E2.jpg)
![适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的多语言人物产品介绍布局提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988108396_vl3wkd_G9ETx2Ub0AATY8H.jpg)
![适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的多语言人物产品介绍布局提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988108589_tjb455_G9EROhUb0AAXwem.jpg)
![适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的多语言人物产品介绍布局提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988110912_owe9p5_G9ETy7Wb0AI-t2D.jpg)

```
language: "{argument name="表示言語" default="ja"}"
# Supported values:
# - ja : Japanese
# - en : English
# - de : German
# - fr : French
# The selected language determines all displayed product text.

product_name: "{argument name="商品名" default="ARBITRARY_PRODUCT_NAME"}"
manufacturer_name: "{argument name="メーカー名" default="ARBITRARY_MANUFACTURER_NAME"}"

subject: >
  The character from reference image A, faithfully preserved in design, proportions,
  facial features, hairstyle, outfit details, and color palette.
  The character is transformed into a highly detailed, photorealistic PVC figure.
  Sculpting style and overall aesthetic are inferred directly from the reference image.
  The figure is presented as a 1/7 scale collectible.

composition: >
  Product introduction layout inferred based on the selected language.
  Vertical composition with a 3:4 aspect ratio.
  A large main visual of the full figure.
  A single, clearly defined product information area containing all textual elements.
  Product name logo and manufacturer name logo are each displayed exactly once.
  Multiple inset close-up panels are included.
  Each inset focuses on a different physical area or feature of the figure.
  No two inset panels depict the same part or the same visual characteristic.
  Inset panels must be visually and conceptually distinct.

action: >
  Static collectible figure pose with no movement.
  Emphasis on sculpt accuracy, proportions, and surface detail.

location: >
  Neutral studio-like environment inferred for product photography.
  Minimal, non-distracting background.

style: >
  Photorealistic product rendering and photography style.
  Artistic tone and mood inferred entirely from the reference image.

camera_lighting: >
  Camera angle and lighting optimized for collectible figure presentation.
  Realistic studio lighting interacting with PVC surfaces.
  Glossy highlights on hair and cl
```

### 9. Nano Banana Pro 社交游戏必杀技制作提示

**Author**: [とすくん](https://x.com/tokyo_Valentine)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: ja

> 一个高度详细、多部分的提示，旨在生成社交游戏特殊招式序列（切入动画、招式名称、伤害显示）的屏幕截图。它严格要求在参考图像的基础上保持角色原有的艺术风格，同时推断出戏剧性效果、UI，以及一个随机的、中二病风格的日文招式名称和伤害值。

![Nano Banana Pro 社交游戏必杀技制作提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988112297_ho7xdx_G9EF-yIbsAAolNZ.jpg)

```
品質: Ultra High Quality / 4K相当 / 高精細 / 高コントラスト
形式: 最新スマートフォン向けゲームの必殺技発動シーンUI
用途: SNSで共有される公式ゲーム級スクリーンショット

────────────────────
【最重要：キャラクター絵柄の完全固定】
・入力イラストのキャラクターの
  顔立ち、目の形、瞳の質感、輪郭、髪型、塗り、色使い、雰囲気を
  一切変更しない
・別人化、別絵師風、画風変化は禁止
・キャラクターは「元イラストの延長線上」として扱う
・描き直し、再デザイン、再解釈は禁止

【推論を許可する範囲】
・推論は以下のみに限定する：
  UI / 文字 / エフェクト / ダメージ数値 / 演出
・キャラクターの外見・年齢感・印象は完全固定
────────────────────

【構図・カメラ】
・胸上〜腰までのアップ構図
・画面の60〜70％をキャラクターが占有
・顔、特に「目」は画面上部または左右に寄せる
・目の周囲には文字・UI・エフェクトを一切配置しない
・全身構図は禁止

────────────────────
【必殺技名（主役・最大表示）】
・画面中央に固定表示
・極太・特大サイズの日本語筆文字
・現在出せる最大サイズ
・文字の一部が画面外にはみ出す
・キャラクターの顔、特に目には絶対に重ねない

【技名の金縁（微調整・重要）】
・金縁は「やや細め」に調整
・縁取りを詰めて文字密度を上げる
・金の発光は抑えめ、黒ベタとのコントラスト重視
・ロゴ感・重量感を優先し、派手さは一段落とす

【必殺技名の生成ルール】
・入力イラストの世界観・属性・雰囲気から
  完全オリジナルの日本語技名を毎回生成
・厨二病的で重厚
・神話、断罪、蒼氷、紅蓮、終焉、機械、神性などの要素を含める
・既存作品名、固有名詞、例文、サンプルは禁止
・「例」「サンプル」「placeholder」等は一切表示しない
────────────────────

【技の威力（変動制・最適化）】
・必殺技の威力は毎回異なる数値を表示する
・ダメージ数値は以下の範囲内でランダムに生成：

  12,000,000 ～ 98,000,000

・最大値固定は禁止
・ゾロ目、カンスト値、完全一致は禁止
・自然で強そうな歪な数値を優先

【ダメージ数値フォント（重量強化）】
・フォントは太く、角張り、重心が低い
・横幅をやや広く、縦に潰しすぎない
・金属的・岩のような質量感
・発光は控えめ、影と立体感で重さを出す
・「数字そのものが重い」印象を与える

【威力の表示構成】
・CRITICAL!! は必須表示
・ダメージ数値は画面中央で最大の存在感
・CRITICAL → 数値 → 技名 の視線導線
────────────────────

【OVERKILL 表示ルール（最重要）】
・OVERKILL表記は一切表示しない
・文字・UI・演出のどこにも使用しない
────────────────────

【キャラクター情報UI】
・レアリティ（UR / LR）
・Lv.MAX
・画面上部に小さく集約
・キャラクターより主張しない

【HP・ゲージ】
・HPバーは下部に細く配置
・HPが0以下であることはゲージ表現のみで伝える
・テキストによる強調は禁止

【その他UI】
・AUTO / SPEED / MENU は画面端に極小配置
・半透明、情報過多にならない設計
────────────────────

【演出方針】
・中央（技名＋ダメージ）のみが激しく動く
・キャラクターの顔・目・表情は静かに保つ
・「絵柄は静、文字と数値は重く、演出は最小限で強い」

【色設計】
・黒 × 金 × 属性色
・顔周辺は落ち着いたトーン
・中央は最大コントラスト
────────────────────

【厳守事項】
・キャラクターの絵柄を絶対に変えない
・目に文字やUIを重ねない
・技名は中央・最大サイズ
・OVERKILLを表示しない
・ダメージ数値を固定しない
・説明文、例文、補足テキストは表示しない
```

[[Identity Preservation]]

### 36. 为头像添加圣诞帽（图像到图像）

**Author**: [katon](https://x.com/hellokaton)  **Date**: 2025-12-24  **Language**: en

> 一个简单、实用的图像到图像生成提示，专门用于为上传的个人资料图片主体添加一顶传统的圣诞老人帽。该提示强调精确保留原始艺术风格、身份和构图，确保帽子与匹配的光照和阴影自然融合。

![为头像添加圣诞帽（图像到图像）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766935985016_no1f9m_G87oN29a0AA3enJ.jpg)
![为头像添加圣诞帽（图像到图像）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766935985209_c3opx4_G87oNogbYAAWvqu.jpg)

```
Using the user-uploaded reference image as the base, add a classic Christmas Santa hat to the subject.

Style match: preserve the original art style exactly (2D/3D/photorealistic/anime/cartoon), keeping identity, facial features, hairstyle, colors, shading, and overall composition unchanged.

Hat design: traditional Santa hat (red felt with subtle fabric texture, white fluffy trim, white pom-pom). Place it naturally on top of the head, aligned to head angle and hairline. Respect perspective, scale, and head shape.

Integration: match the existing lighting, shadows, highlights, linework, and rendering style. Add realistic contact shadows where the hat touches hair/forehead. Do not alter the face, hair, background, clothing, or any other elements.

Output: square (1:1) avatar, crisp and clear at small profile-picture size.
```

**Author**: [katon](https://x.com/hellokaton)  **Date**: 2025-12-24  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于在 Gemini 上使用 Nano Banana Pro 进行图像到图像的生成，旨在创建电影般的高端韩流时尚杂志肖像。它严格保留了上传参考图像中人物的身份，同时应用了戏剧性的午夜氛围、特定的光照（包括虹彩棱镜效果）和“嘘”的手势。

    },

        "composition": "Extreme close-up editorial portrait (head fills the frame), eyes near the upper third, slight turn toward camera, tight crop from forehead to chin with the hand entering frame from below.",
        "action": "Perform a 'shh' gesture: one index finger held vertically and gently pressed to the center of the lips. Finger pad lightly compresses the lip surface; lips slightly parted with glossy lip oil; subtle contact shadow where finger meets lips. Expression calm, mysterious, and intimate; eyelids relaxed.",
        "location": "Dark studio backdrop, midnight mood, no visible set elements.",
        "style": "Midnight K-fashion editorial, cinematic high-end beauty photography, clean but dramatic, premium magazine-grade retouching (natural pores, not plastic).",

            "shot_type": "beauty close-up",
            "lens": "85mm prime",
            "aperture": "f/1.8",
            "focus": "sharp focus on the eyes and lips; finger also sharp at the contact point; soft falloff to hair edges",
            "depth_of_field": "shallow"
        },
        "lighting": {
            "base": "low-key studio lighting with deep blacks",
            "key_light": "soft key from camera-right, slightly above eye level",
            "fill": "very subtle fill from camera-left to keep shadows readable",
            "signature_effect": "a diagonal iridescent prism light band across the face ({argument name="prism color gradient" default="cyan-to-violet gradient"}), like a diffraction filter or gel projection; crisp edge with gentle falloff",

            "subtle glitter/metallic shimmer on eyelids",

### 40. 美妆博主圣诞妆容教程界面

**Author**: [松果先森](https://x.com/songguoxiansen)  **Date**: 2025-12-23  **Language**: zh

> 一个高度具体的提示，用于生成一个垂直的社交媒体故事设计（9:16 宽高比），模拟美妆博主的圣诞妆容教程界面。它要求严格复制参考人物的面部，呈现“驯鹿甜酷妆”造型，并在完成的妆容上用红色笔标记，以对应底部 5 个详细化妆步骤的水平滚动预览，将商业摄影质量与 UI 设计元素相结合。

![美妆博主圣诞妆容教程界面](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936032353_vbxknk_G829rIEbIAAsToc.jpg)

```
竖屏社交媒体故事设计 (9:16 宽高比)，美妆博主圣诞妆容教程界面。背景为柔和的高级感粉色渐变，营造甜美梦幻氛围。
核心视觉：
人物一致性（最高权重）： 画面中央展示一位亚洲女性美妆博主，面部特征、五官及发型必须严格、完美地复刻上传的参考图片人物。
妆容与配饰： 极度精致的“圣诞麋鹿甜酷妆”。眼妆为红棕色晕染，面部有白色小鹿斑点，头戴毛绒驯鹿角发箍。
红笔标记与步骤对应（逻辑核心）： 在右侧完妆人物的面部，使用醒目的红色墨水笔引出5条指示线，分别指向妆容的5个关键部位，并按顺序标注中文：1. 眼影；2. 金色闪片；3. 睫毛；4. 鹿系腮红；5. 饱满红唇。
排版布局：
顶部： 中文标题“圣诞妆容教程”，搭配口红图标。副标题“麋鹿少女妆 甜酷风”。
中部（对比区）： 左右分屏设计。左侧为该人物“素颜”，右侧为“完妆”。中间用虚线和剪刀图标连接。
下部（强关联步骤预览区）： 设置横向滑动的圆角卡片栏，展示5个与面部标记严格对应的步骤图：
卡片1：眼部涂抹眼影的特写；
卡片2：用手指点缀金色闪片的特写；
卡片3：夹睫毛或刷睫毛的特写；
卡片4：面颊扫腮红和画鹿斑的特写；
卡片5：涂抹红色口红的嘴唇特写。 每张卡片左上角需清晰标注数字1-5，与面部红笔标记的序号呼应。
底部（互动区）： “上滑看完整教程”箭头，“点击查看同款产品”按钮，点赞与收藏图标。
风格： 高清商业摄影质感结合UI设计，光影通透，色彩鲜艳，肤质细腻真实，时尚杂志排版风格。 --ar 9:16
```

### 45. 生日庆祝霓虹海报拼贴提示

**Author**: [𝗦𝗮𝗻𝗶𝗮](https://x.com/saniaspeaks_)  **Date**: 2025-12-22  **Language**: en

    "body_preservation": "{argument name="body preservation" default="exact"}",

    "no_body_modification": true
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "{argument name="gender" default="female"}",
    "age": "{argument name="age" default="young adult"}",

    "pose": "{argument name="pose" default="slightly angled mirror selfie pose, relaxed shoulders, natural posture"}",

      "color": "{argument name="hair color" default="dark brown"}",

      "texture": "{argument name="hair texture" default="smooth and realistic"}"
    },

    }

### 53. 逼真的 MacBook 屏幕 POV 自拍提示词

**Author**: [Zaylee](https://x.com/zayleeai)  **Date**: 2025-12-19  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 设计的复杂 JSON 提示词，用于图像到图像的生成，重点在于创建一个超现实的 POV 视角，向下俯视 MacBook 屏幕。屏幕上显示的是 Photo Booth 的实时预览，主体（其身份严格保留自输入照片）身处昏暗的卧室中，背景播放着 Spotify。该提示词强调真实感细节，如 RGB 像素网格、灰尘和自然噪点，模拟的是对屏幕拍摄的照片，而非屏幕截图。

"A hyper-realistic, extreme close-up beauty portrait of a stunning woman. She is raising her arm to cover the left side of her face, wearing a vibrant red ribbed-knit sweater. Her pose shows her leaning out of a train window, with both arms resting comfortably on the window frame and her upper body slightly leaned forward in a relaxed, cozy posture.
She has dark brown straight hair worn loose and slightly tucked under a white knitted winter beanie with a soft knit texture. Her makeup is natural winter-style, featuring an even fair skin tone, light blush, soft eyeliner, natural lashes, and subtle pink lips. She is wearing a cream or off-white cozy winter sweater made of soft, warm knit fabric suitable for cold weather.
The scene is set inside a red panoramic train traveling through snowy alpine mountains. The background includes snow-covered pine trees, mountain slopes blanketed in snow, curving red train cars visible behind her, and thick snow piled along the tracks, clearly conveying a winter landscape. Lighting is natural cold daylight with soft diffusion, cool winter tones, gentle highlights on the face, and natural shadows.
The overall style is a cinematic travel portrait with a DSLR photography look, moderate depth of field that keeps the subject sharp while preserving scenic background detail, and a peaceful, cozy, adventurous winter travel mood. Use high-resolution rendering with realistic skin texture, high detail, and cool winter color grading with soft contrast, maintaining strict identity lock to the reference image throughout."

Prompt 3:
"Create A hyper-realistic person (Retro vintage, grainy but bright aesthetic. A girl(face exactly same as the reference image) wearing a perfect red wine colored red frock, holding a A bunch of 10-12 flowers of roses in her hands. The style feels like a 90s movie, romantic, wind blowing girl. She is standing against a solid wall with deep shadows and dramatic contrast, mysterious and artistic atmosphere."

### 58. 维多利亚哥特式皇家肖像杂志封面提示

**Author**: [松果先森](https://x.com/songguoxiansen)  **Date**: 2025-12-19  **Language**: zh

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的极其详细、多部分的提示，用于生成一张 9:16 垂直、写实风格的杂志封面照片，风格为“维多利亚哥特式皇家”。它要求 100% 保留上传的面部参考的身份，特定的重型维多利亚宫廷服饰，以伦敦地标为背景，电影级灯光，复杂的色彩矩阵选择，以及适合杂志封面的特定姿势。

![维多利亚哥特式皇家肖像杂志封面提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766238189353_t1rx5n_G8diWGcakAckiYD.jpg)

```
生成一张 9:16 竖版「维多利亚哥特皇室」写实照片：以我上传的 FACE_REF 为人物身份参考，100%还原五官与骨相；人物身穿“维多利亚时代（19世纪）宫廷礼服方向”的重工礼服（紧身胸衣、大裙撑、蕾丝/天鹅绒、皇室珠宝），在伦敦塔桥或威斯敏斯特宫（大本钟）旁拍摄。画面具备《Harper’s Bazaar》级别的摄影、造型与封面设计，保持杂志的一贯设计风格（中英文设计）。

【INPUTS | 输入】
FACE_REF：我上传的人物五官参考图（身份锁定）

【ABSOLUTE PRIORITY | 身份锁定（最高优先级）】
100%还原 FACE_REF 的五官与骨相：眼距、鼻梁鼻翼、唇形、下颌线、颧骨结构完全一致，不得漂移。
真实皮肤质感：可见细微纹理与毛孔，不要过度磨皮与网红化。
成年女性形象（adult）。

【SHOT TYPE | 景别二选一（由模型随机选其一，且必须真实统一）】
A) 半身封面：胸口到腰上方，珠宝、蕾丝领口与眼神最清晰（主推）
B) 全身封面：从头到脚完整呈现巨大的裙撑轮廓与伦敦地标的结合，透视感强（备选）
（无论A/B：都必须保持“封面构图”，有留白空间给排版，但不要撕纸/手绘效果。）

【LOCATION | 场景（英国伦敦）】
伦敦地标：泰晤士河畔，背景是宏伟的哥特式建筑威斯敏斯特宫（大本钟）或 伦敦塔桥的塔楼。
天气二选一（随机）：1) 伦敦雾霭（经典的雾都质感，光线柔和神秘） 2) 阴雨方歇（地面湿润反光，天空呈铅灰色）
背景干净：无游客、无现代标识、无手机状态栏UI、无水印字幕。

【LIGHTING & CAMERA | 摄影质感（杂志级）】
镜头感：85mm人像质感（半身）或 50mm/70mm（全身），浅景深，眼睛最清晰。
光线：阴天漫射光 + 戏剧性补光（强调面部结构）；钻石/宝石有真实火彩；天鹅绒质感深邃。
色彩：高级电影感，低饱和度的蓝灰环境色与服装的深色调（红/蓝/黑）形成哥特美学；整体干净、通透、贵气。

【WARDROBE | 维多利亚宫廷礼服（重工、塑形、繁复细节）】
目标审美：“蜂腰、大裙摆、层叠蕾丝、重磅天鹅绒、皇冠、女王气场”。

轮廓与层次（X型剪裁）
上身：结构感极强的紧身胸衣（Corset），方领或高领，泡泡袖或羊腿袖
下身：巨大的裙撑（Crinoline 或 Bustle），后腰部有明显的堆叠设计，裙摆拖地
装饰：大量的荷叶边、蝴蝶结、垂坠的流苏
面料与工艺（重手艺必须“看得见”）
主面料：重磅丝绒、塔夫绸、尚蒂伊蕾丝（Chantilly Lace）
主要工艺：珠绣、金线刺绣、缎带编织
纹样主题：大马士革纹（Damask）、玫瑰、蓟花（苏格兰象征）、佩斯利纹
细节：蕾丝手套、颈饰（Choker）、勋章/胸针
头面（皇室珠宝头饰）
核心结构：维多利亚式小王冠（Tiara）或 羽毛头饰
装饰：钻石、蓝宝石、珍珠
耳饰/颈饰：极度夸张的钻石项链、耳坠

【COLOR MATRIX | 颜色矩阵搭配（必须执行，且必须“皇室深色”）】
（维多利亚晚期的深沉奢华）
从以下三套“主色方案”中随机选 1 套作为【底色/大面积主面料色】。

Scheme G（皇室蓝底）：
底色：深宝蓝/午夜蓝（丝绒质感）
刺绣/装饰：银色蕾丝、钻石、蓝宝石
Scheme A（维多利亚红底）：
底色：酒红/勃艮第红（深沉热情）
刺绣/装饰：黑色蕾丝、金色刺绣、红宝石
Scheme R（丧服黑底）：
底色：墨黑（Black Jet，极度哥特）
刺绣/装饰：黑色串珠、黑色蕾丝、少量金色或银色提亮

【颜色执行规则】
色彩要深沉浓郁，体现“日不落”的威严和哥特式的神秘。

【POSE | 封面姿态（威严、僵直、女王感）】
半身：下巴微扬，眼神冷峻，一手轻抚项链
全身：站姿挺拔（像肖像画一样），双手交叠在裙撑上，气场压倒一切
表情：严肃、高傲、不可一世；绝对不笑（维多利亚风格）。

【OUTPUT | 输出】
1 张 9:16 竖版写实杂志封面级照片
随机：半身 or 全身（A/B二选一）
随机：雾霭 or 阴雨（天气二选一）
随机：宝蓝 / 酒红 / 墨黑（颜色矩阵三选一）
造型：维多利亚宫廷礼服方向 + 皇冠/Choker + 紧身胸衣大裙撑 + 丝绒蕾丝
```

[[Identity Preservation]] [[Cinematic Lighting]] [[Magazine Cover]]

### 62. 将物体冻结在逼真的冰块中

**Author**: [Recraft](https://x.com/recraftai)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，旨在将上传的主体（人物或物体）完全置于一个巨大的、超逼真的矩形冰块内部，同时严格保持原始姿势、比例、背景和光照，并着重于逼真的冰块纹理和折射效果。

```
"Place the entire subject from the uploaded photo fully inside a large, ultra-realistic rectangular block of ice. Do not change the pose, scale, camera angle, composition, background, or lighting. Preserve all original clothing, accessories, facial features, colors, and details exactly. Do not stylize or recolor the subject. The ice should be crystal clear with internal frost, frozen cracks, trapped air bubbles, and subtle imperfections, with realistic refraction so the subject appears deeply encased—not on the surface. The block must rest solidly on the ground with scattered ice shards around the base, matching the scene’s lighting. Maintain accurate shadows and reflections. No melting or dripping. Ultra-photorealistic, cinematic realism."
```

```
{
  "task": "image_to_image_style_transfer",

  "prompt": "Create a hyper-real 3D studio composition that recreates the main subject from the provided image as a fragmented stone assemblage. Material look: fragmented slate + sandstone shards with chiseled edges, crisp fractures, visible stone grain, micro-scratches, and realistic roughness. Color palette: predominantly dark slate with subtle warm-ochre sandstone accents. Lighting: soft studio key light from top-left, gentle fill, subtle contact shadows under each shard, realistic ambient occlusion in crevices, clean reflections kept minimal. Background: minimal off-white seamless backdrop, no texture. Framing: centered, clean, straight-on, subject fully readable. Add a few tiny debris chips floating or resting near the base for depth. Preserve the subject’s identity, proportions, and recognizable silhouette from the input image while transforming all surfaces into stone fragments. Hyper-real, high detail, sharp focus, 8k render quality.",
  "negative_prompt": "text, typography, logo, watermark, signature, extra props, busy background, fog, heavy bloom, cartoon, illustration, lowpoly, plastic, metal, glossy paint, melted shapes, merged fragments, unreadable subject, blur, noise, low resolution, oversharpening halos, distorted face/body, extra limbs, deformed geometry",
  "output": {
    "aspect_ratio": "use_input_aspect_ratio",
    "background": "off_white",
    "camera": {
      "angle": "straight_on",
      "framing": "centered",
      "distance": "medium"
    }
  },

    "lighting_preset": "soft_studio_top_left",
    "shadow_intensity": "subtle",

  }
}

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 创建一个详细的提示，用于从上传的图像生成电影风格的 3x3 联系表。该提示要求保留运动员的身份、服装和垫子，但将环境更改为户外、中午的场景。提示中还指定了九种不同锻炼动作的精确姿势和标签，以确保所有帧的风格和构图保持一致。

![电影级 3x3 训练联系表生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237880326_h3zr64_G8cyfilWYAAuMqZ.jpg)

```
Create a cinematic 3×3 contact sheet from the uploaded image. Keep the same athlete, face, body proportions, workout lingerie, workout mat, and workout location across all nine frames. Update the environment to an outdoor setting. Set time of day to midday with natural overhead sunlight. The workout mat stays identical in color, position, texture, and orientation in every frame. Use a mix of wide shots and close-up shots. Apply consistent cinematic color grading, soft contrast, and film-style lighting adapted to bright midday conditions. Every frame appears as a film still from the same outdoor workout session.

Environment details
• Outdoor location such as {argument name="outdoor location" default="rooftop, park, terrace, or open concrete space"}
• Clear midday sky
• Bright natural light from above
• Soft natural shadows under the athlete
• No background changes between frames

Workout lingerie details
• Fitted sleeveless workout top
• High-waist compression leggings
• Seamless matte athletic fabric
• Wavy {argument name="lingerie pattern color" default="purple, green, and blue"} pattern
• Practical training-focused fit
• Lightweight workout shoes
• Stable sole for balance

For each cell
• Show the correct exercise pose matching the workout label
• Add a workout exercise label at the top left
• Match label text exactly to the exercise shown
• Place text on a solid black background
• Keep a clear margin from the image edge
• Add padding inside the label
• Use a small corner radius
• Use clean sans-serif text in white
• Keep label size consistent across all cells
• Add a 1px solid black border around each cell

Top row
• Squat, athlete performing a squat
• Slow Burpees, athlete mid controlled burpee
• Knee Tuck Crunch, athlete performing knee tuck crunch

Middle row
• Reach Through, athlete performing reach through
• Russian Twist, athlete seated performing Russian twist
• Bird Dog, athlete performing bird dog on the mat

Bottom row
• Superman Hold, athlete holding superman position
• Jumping Jacks, athlete mid jumping jack
• Lateral Steps, athlete performing lateral side steps

Rules
• No identity change
• Same workout lingerie across all frames
• Same workout mat across all frames
• No body shape change
• Outdoor location stays consistent
• No added equipment
• Same lighting direction across all frames
• Film still style, no collage

### 73. Nano Banana Pro 的图像转雪雕提示词

**Author**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: ja

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的高度详细的提示，用于将参考图像转换为巨大的雪雕，强调雕塑必须是纯白色雪，不带任何颜料，细节仅通过阴影和浮雕来表现。该提示包括雕塑风格、姿势以及标题牌等周围元素的具体规则。

![Nano Banana Pro 的图像转雪雕提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237936652_zbbi6o_G8ckB-wakAMXPNe.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 的图像转雪雕提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237937740_yzo9l0_G8ckDNHakAAYpSn.jpg)

```
【設定】
[キャラクターの外見] = {argument name="キャラクターの外見" default="髪をツインテールにした黒いマントの少女とセーラー服の少女"}
[タイトル] = {argument name="タイトル" default="二人は仲良し"}

変換のルール:
- 日本の雪まつりの会場で撮影された、[キャラクター]を模した高さ3メートルほどの巨大な雪像の写真。
- 重要：この像は全て「真っ白な雪」だけで作られている。塗装は一切されておらず、色は完全に白一色である。
- キャラクターの目や服の模様は、雪の凹凸と陰影だけで表現されている。
- 雪像は、背景にある巨大な雪の壁に半分埋まるように彫刻された「高浮き彫り」のスタイル。
- キャラクターは躍動感のあるダイナミックなダンスのポーズをとっている。
- 雪像の足元には雪の台座があり、台座の表面には「[タイトル]」という文字が雪に深く彫り込まれている。
- 雪像のすぐ横の雪面には、参照用の「カラーイラスト」と「[タイトル]」が印刷された四角い立て看板が設置されている（看板だけはカラフル）。
- アングルは、人の目の高さから斜めに見上げる構図。
- 雪の表面は少しざらついた圧雪の質感。冬の自然光。

アートスタイル:
- 昼間の自然光、冬の澄んだ空気、4K画質
```

### 79. 个性化壁画工作室肖像

**Author**: [D. Humann](https://x.com/dhumann)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张高分辨率的影棚照片，照片中的主体在自己大型风格化矢量艺术壁画前摆姿势。该提示强调摄影写实主义、受控的电影级灯光，以及真实主体与彩绘壁画之间的清晰区别，并要求提供参考图像以保留身份。

![个性化壁画工作室肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237825336_lcrz0m_G8bGrc2aAAAdjzQ.jpg)

```
Create a high-resolution studio photograph featuring THE_SUBJECT, using the uploaded photo as a strict visual reference for identity. THE_SUBJECT’s facial features, skin tone, body proportions, hairstyle, facial hair, and overall appearance must match the reference image exactly, with no reinterpretation or stylization of THE_SUBJECT. 

THE_SUBJECT is standing naturally and casually, leaning against a plain concrete or plaster studio wall. THE_SUBJECT is photographed as a real person in a real studio environment — this is a photographic image, not an illustration.

Painted directly onto the wall behind THE_SUBJECT is a large-scale mural depicting THE_SUBJECT’s face and upper body. The mural is a stylized vector-art portrait of THE_SUBJECT, clearly recognizable as the same person, rendered in bold graphic shapes, clean edges, and modern illustrative color blocking. The mural is significantly larger than life-size and occupies most of the wall surface.

THE_SUBJECT’s real body partially overlaps and obscures the mural, reinforcing depth and scale, while still making it immediately clear that the mural represents THE_SUBJECT. The mural must remain visibly painted on the wall, not floating, not projected, and not a digital overlay.

Lighting is controlled studio lighting with a cinematic feel: soft but directional, illuminating both THE_SUBJECT and the mural evenly, with subtle contrast and color separation that allows the real subject and the painted mural to coexist clearly in the same physical space.

The final image should feel like a professional studio portrait photographed in front of a custom mural wall — realistic, grounded, and visually cohesive — with a clear distinction between the real human subject and the stylized painted portrait behind them.
```

### 82. 90 年代自拍情绪网格与身份锁

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2025-12-17  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的高度结构化提示，要求生成一个 3x3 网格拼贴画，其中包含同一人物（身份锁定自参考图像）的九张特写自拍。所有自拍需保持一致的背景和服装，但每张照片中的面部表情/情绪各不相同（例如，调情、愤怒、哭泣、开心）。

![90 年代自拍情绪网格与身份锁](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042055311_c2f3ov_G8ZmVkyWgAEy08Q.jpg)

```
{
  "request_metadata": {
    "model": "Nano Banana Pro",
    "content_type": "photorealistic_90s_selfie_emotion_grid",
    "quality_preset": "ultra",
    "format_aspect_ratio": "1:1",
    "output": "3x3_grid"
  },

  "layout": {
    "type": "3x3_grid",
    "description": "Same person in all 9 frames. Keep identity locked. Same room, same curtain backdrop, same outfit, same lighting. Only facial expression/emotion + micro-gesture changes per frame.",
    "frame_labels": [
      "1) Flirty bite + wink",
      "2) Happy smile",
      "3) Angry",
      "4) Crying",
      "5) Blowing a kiss",
      "6) Playful wink",
      "7) Surprised",
      "8) Serious/neutral",
      "9) Smirk/confident"
    ]
  },

  "source": {
    "mode": "image_reference",
    "reference_images": {
      "primary": "base_person_image"
    },
    "preserve": {
      "same_person": true,
      "identity_lock": true,
      "keep_face": true,
      "keep_hair": true,
      "keep_outfit": true,
      "keep_skin_tone": true,
      "keep_freckles": true,
      "keep_eye_color": true,
      "keep_earrings": true
    }
  },

  "global_scene": {
    "shot_type": "close-up selfie portrait",
    "camera_pose": "right hand holding the camera for selfie, arm slightly forward",
    "body_pose": "body tilted slightly to the right",
    "environment": "a room with a grayish-white curtain backdrop, soft out-of-focus folds",
    "lighting": {
      "type": "natural_window_light",
      "direction": "front",
      "quality": "soft but bright",
      "notes": "keep consistent across all 9 frames; no lighting changes between frames"
    },
    "style": {
      "look": "90s camera selfie",
      "grain": "subtle film grain",
      "flash_feel": "mild on-camera flash feel (soft pop, not harsh)",
      "realism": "authentic candid realism"
    },
    "quality": {
      "detail": "high detail",
      "skin_texture": "natural skin texture, visible pores, realistic freckles",
      "retouching": "minimal; avoid smoothing/beauty filter"
    },
    "composition_lock": {
      "keep_framing": true,
      "keep_camera_distance": true,
      "keep_head_position": "only micro-variations allowed",
      "keep_background": true
    }
  },

  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "age_group": "young_adult",
    "identity": "EXACT same face as reference (do not change facial structure, eyes, nose, lips, jawline)",
    "hair": "dark brown with highlights, high messy bun, bangs circling the forehead",
    "accessories": "diamond hoop earrings",
    "skin_details": "freckles around nose and cheekbones",
    "makeup": {
      "style": "natural",
      "blush": "subtle pink",
      "eyeliner": "defined cat-eye",
      "lashes": "curled",
      "lip": "glossy nude",
      "eyes": "brownish-green"
    },
    "outfit": "strapless black knit mini dress"
  },

  "frames": [
    {
      "id": 1,
      "emotion": "flirtatious",
      "expression_action": "biting her index finger g"
    }
  ]
}
```

### 83. 电影烛光美人像编辑提示

```
{
  "mode": "image_edit",

### 84. 从参考图像生成电影级联系表

**Author**: [DStudioproject](https://x.com/D_studioproject)  **Date**: 2025-12-17  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多步骤提示，旨在根据上传的参考图像生成一个连贯的 3x3 电影式分镜头脚本。它指示模型内化场景和主体，然后创建一系列从不同距离和角度拍摄的图像，同时在主体、位置、光线和情感基调方面保持绝对的一致性。

![从参考图像生成电影级联系表](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042091407_mbl36v_G8Y2JURa0AAf2eA.jpg)

```
Study the uploaded image carefully and fully internalize the scene: the subject’s appearance, clothing, posture, emotional state, and the surrounding environment. Treat this moment as a single frozen point in time.
Create a cinematic image set that feels like a photographer methodically explored this exact moment from multiple distances and angles, without changing anything about the subject or location.
All images must clearly belong to the same scene, captured under the same lighting conditions, weather, and atmosphere. Nothing in the world changes — only the camera position and framing evolve.
The emotional tone should remain consistent throughout the set, subtly expressed through posture, gaze, and micro-expressions rather than exaggerated acting.
Begin by observing the subject within the environment from afar, letting the surroundings dominate the frame and establish scale and mood.
Gradually move closer, allowing the subject’s full presence to emerge, then narrowing attention toward body language and facial expression.
End with intimate perspectives that reveal small but meaningful details — texture, touch, or eye focus — before shifting perspective above and below the subject to suggest reflection, vulnerability, or quiet resolve.
Across the sequence:
Wider views should emphasize space and atmosphere
Mid-range views should emphasize posture and emotional context
Close views should isolate feeling and detail
Perspective shifts (low and high angles) should feel purposeful and cinematic, not decorative
Depth of field must behave naturally: distant views remain mostly sharp, while closer frames introduce shallow focus and gentle background separation.
The final result should read as a cohesive 3×3 cinematic contact sheet, as if selected from a single roll of film documenting one emotional moment from multiple viewpoints.
No text, symbols, signage, watermarks, numbers, or graphic elements may appear anywhere in the images.
Photorealistic rendering, cinematic color grading, and consistent visual realism are mandatory.
```

[[Identity Preservation]]

---

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 提供一个高度详细的提示，请求一张年轻女性的写实艺术工作室肖像（基于参考照片），姿势为半侧身，身穿复古浪漫的象牙色连衣裙，强调电影般的低调布光和神秘自信的表情。

![复古连衣裙中的艺术微光人像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042054640_guns6c_G8WxYSUaMAEpLD-.jpg)

```
A realistic fine art studio portrait of a slim young woman (face identical to the attached reference photo) with pale skin and naturally dark, curly hair at shoulder length. She is lying on a soft surface in a semi-side pose, her body placed diagonally within the frame. One arm is bent and placed behind her head, while the other arm is gently raised with a relaxed wrist and graceful fingers. Her legs are softly bent, creating flowing, elegant body lines. Her head faces straight toward the camera with her chin slightly lifted.

Her facial expression is calm, confident, and subtly mysterious. Her gaze looks directly into the camera, with naturally thick eyebrows. Her lips are warm red with soft, classic makeup. There is no smile, giving a strong yet poetic impression.

She wears an ivory white vintage–romantic style dress with short puff sleeves, featuring delicate lace and fine embroidery details on the bodice. The satin or silk fabric appears soft and drapes naturally along her body with gentle folds. The fabric texture is clearly visible yet smooth.

Lighting: Soft, cinematic low-key lighting. A single diffused light source from the side–top direction softly illuminates the face, chest, and folds of the dress. Gentle highlights create a glowing effect on the fabric and skin, while deep yet smooth shadows envelop the sides of the body and background. No harsh light. Medium contrast with very smooth shadow transitions, creating an intimate and classic atmosphere.

Background: A plain dark cushioned background in deep greenish-black, without details, with a natural vignette around the edges of the frame to enhance focus on the subject.

Visual style: Fine art portrait photography, vintage cinematic, painterly realism, romantic gothic, old master inspired, classic and dramatic yet soft mood.

Technical details: Shallow depth of field, sharp focus on the face, clear fabric details, slight soft focus, fine grain, cinematic color grading, muted colors, high quality, no excessive modern effects.

Negative Prompt: stiff pose, harsh lighting, overly bright colors, HDR, ultra sharp, modern style, modern clothing, busy background, modern makeup.
```

### 101. 唐朝女皇登上巴黎时尚杂志封面提示

**Author**: [松果先森](https://x.com/songguoxiansen)  **Date**: 2025-12-17  **Language**: zh

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的极其详细的多段提示，用于生成一张 9:16 垂直、逼真的时尚杂志封面照片。照片中的人物面部特征必须与参考图片 100% 一致，身着华丽的唐代宫廷服饰（齐胸襦裙、大袖、牡丹图案、金色饰品），并在巴黎埃菲尔铁塔的背景下拍摄。该提示详细说明了灯光、色彩矩阵（唐代色彩）、姿势（自信的女皇）和杂志级别的构图。

![唐朝女皇登上巴黎时尚杂志封面提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042130660_ee2m3t_G8Wvo8sa4AkLDOE.jpg)

```
生成一张 9:16 竖版「大唐盛世与巴黎」写实照片：以我上传的 FACE_REF 为人物身份参考，100%还原五官与骨相；人物身穿“唐代（盛唐）宫廷贵妃方向”的重工礼服（齐胸衫裙、大袖衫、牡丹纹样、金饰），在巴黎埃菲尔铁塔下的特罗卡德罗广场或塞纳河畔拍摄。画面具备COSMO时尚杂志级别的摄影、造型与封面设计，保持杂志的一贯设计风格（英文设计）。

【INPUTS | 输入】 FACE_REF：我上传的人物五官参考图（身份锁定）

【ABSOLUTE PRIORITY | 身份锁定（最高优先级）】 100%还原 FACE_REF 的五官与骨相：脸型、容貌、眼距、鼻梁鼻翼、唇形、下颌线、颧骨结构完全一致，不得漂移。 真实皮肤质感：可见细微纹理与毛孔，不要过度磨皮与网红化。 成年女性形象。

【SHOT TYPE | 景别二选一（由模型随机选其一，且必须真实统一）】 A) 半身封面：胸口到腰上方，头面与上身刺绣最清晰，眼睛对焦最锐利（主推） B) 全身封面：从头到脚完整呈现层叠礼服与裙摆纹样，铁塔的钢结构透视更强（备选） （无论A/B：都必须保持“封面构图”，有留白空间给排版，但不要撕纸/手绘效果。）

【LOCATION | 场景（巴黎埃菲尔铁塔）】 巴黎埃菲尔铁塔：经典的钢结构塔身背景。天气二选一（随机）：1) 巴黎阴雨（地面微湿，光线柔和高级灰色调，时尚感强） 2) 绚丽黄昏（夕阳余晖，金色光影，浪漫氛围） 背景干净：无游客、无现代标识、无手机状态栏UI、无水印字幕、无护栏。

【LIGHTING & CAMERA | 摄影质感（杂志级）】 镜头感：85mm人像质感（半身）或 50mm/70mm（全身），浅景深，眼睛最清晰。 光线：自然光（强调环境光） + 电影级补光；金饰有真实高光但不爆；丝绸光泽清晰可辨。 色彩：高级电影感，法式米灰/蓝灰色调与唐代服装的“红绿金”配色形成强烈视觉张力；整体干净、通透、质感厚。

【WARDROBE | 唐代宫廷礼服（丰腴、飘逸、色彩浓烈）】 目标审美：“金饰华丽、面靥花钿、齐胸裙、披帛飘逸、大红大绿大金、极度张扬”。

轮廓与层次（必须体现唐代特征） 内层：诃子（抹胸），露出颈部与上胸肌肤（唐代开放风气） 中层：对襟短衫（直领），材质透明轻薄（罗/纱） 外层：大袖衫（极宽大的袖子，拖地），像翅膀一样张开 装饰：披帛（长长的丝带），挽在手臂间，随风飘舞 下装：齐胸破裙（裙腰系在胸口，裙摆宽大，多色拼接或印花） 面料与工艺（重手艺必须“看得见”） 主面料：丝绸、织锦、印金纱（轻盈与厚重结合） 主要工艺：印染（蜡染/夹路）、金线刺绣、织金 纹样主题（适配大唐）：宝相花、缠枝牡丹、瑞兽（狮子/麒麟）、团花（图案巨大、饱满） 细节：花钿（额头红色装饰）、面靥（嘴角红点）、臂钗（大臂上的金属饰品） 头面（唐代雍容华贵头饰） 核心结构：高耸的发髻（云髻/坠马髻），插戴大朵牡丹花（真花或绢花） 装饰：金梳背（插在发髻上的金梳子）、步摇（走动摇曳）、金钗 耳饰：贵重金玉

【COLOR MATRIX | 颜色矩阵搭配（必须执行，且必须“浓烈唐风”）】 （调整为唐代流行色：红绿撞色、金碧辉煌） 从以下三套“主色方案”中随机选 1 套作为【底色/大面积主面料色】。

Scheme G（石青/翠绿底）： 底色：{argument name="底色1" default="翠绿/石青"}（常用的间色） 刺绣/印染：茜红、金色、橘黄、米白 Scheme A（牡丹红底）： 底色：{argument name="底色2" default="牡丹红/石榴红"}（最经典的唐风） 刺绣/印染：金色、翠绿、宝蓝、紫 Scheme R（紫底）： 底色：{argument name="底色3" default="紫/葡萄色"}（高贵） 刺绣/印染：金色、朱红、草绿、银

【颜色执行规则】 色彩对比要强烈，体现盛唐气象，但整体色调要统一在高级感中。

【POSE | 封面姿态（自信、舒展、女王感）】 半身：微昂头，眼神睥睨，一手轻抚发髻或披帛 全身：双臂张开带动大袖衫和披帛，展现服装的体积感，气场全开 表情：自信、张扬、妩媚、大方；不要羞涩。

【OUTPUT | 输出】 1 张 9:16 竖版写实杂志封面级照片 随机：半身 or 全身（A/B二选一） 随机：阴雨 or 黄昏（天气二选一） 随机：翠绿 / 牡丹红 / 紫（颜色矩阵三选一） 造型：唐代宫廷礼服方向 + 牡丹花/金梳头面 + 齐胸大袖 + 披帛
```

### 102. 巴黎电影风格塔楼肖像，保留身份特征

**Author**: [𝗦𝗮𝗻𝗶𝗮](https://x.com/saniaspeaks_)  **Date**: 2025-12-17  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于 Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro，旨在生成一张超现实、电影级的女性肖像，她自信地站立在一座著名的巴黎塔顶。该提示严格要求保留上传图片中的身份，并聚焦于金色的日光下巴黎的壮丽全景。

![巴黎电影风格塔楼肖像，保留身份特征](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042024918_1dmuvy_G8Vwf3ea4AI7thD.jpg)

```
{
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",
  "style": "hyper-realistic, cinematic, awe-inspiring",
  "identity_preservation": {
    "use_uploaded_image": true,
    "alter_face": false,
    "notes": "Use the uploaded image as a strict reference. Do not edit or alter the woman’s facial features, body proportions, or natural appearance in any way."
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "age": 22,
    "height": "1.60m",
    "pose": {
      "stance": "standing confidently at the very top of a famous tower in Paris",
      "body_language": "upright, open, embracing the view",
      "expression": "calm, free, inspired"
    },
    "wardrobe": {
      "top": "white t-shirt",
      "accessories": [
        "black wristwatch"
      ]
    }
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "top of a famous Parisian tower",
    "background": {
      "cityscape": [
        "Paris skyline",
        "Eiffel Tower in the distance",
        "classic Parisian rooftops",
        "winding streets below"
      ],
      "atmosphere": "soft atmospheric haze adding depth"
    }
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "golden daylight",
    "effect": [
      "warm sunlight across the city",
      "natural highlights and shadows",
      "cinematic depth"
    ]
  },
  "camera": {
    "angle": "wide-angle, slightly low perspective",
    "effect": "makes the subject appear majestic and free",
    "aspect_ratio": "16:9"
  },
  "mood": {
    "tone": [
      "liberating",
      "cinematic",
      "awe-inspiring"
    ]
  },
  "quality": {
    "realism": "ultra-realistic",
    "detail_level": "high cinematic detail"
  },
  "output_goal": "Create a hyper-realistic cinematic image of a young woman standing atop a Parisian tower, preserving her exact identity while showcasing a majestic panoramic view of Paris under golden daylight."
}
```

### 103. 波西米亚风格卧室中坦率的镜子自拍结构化 JSON 提示

**Author**: [ChromeRuby](https://x.com/chromerubbdx)  **Date**: 2025-12-17  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细 JSON 提示，用于生成一张年轻女性在昏暗、杂乱、波西米亚风格卧室中拍摄的坦率镜面自拍照。该提示根据参考图像指定了拍摄对象的身份、发型、服装、姿势（盘腿坐着，手持智能手机）、环境细节（复古梳妆台、白色金属凳），以及具有颗粒感和柔和色彩的电影般摄影风格。

![波西米亚风格卧室中坦率的镜子自拍结构化 JSON 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042195234_aj4oo4_G8Va__kXoAMZGNM.jpg)

```
{
  "detailed_prompts": {
    "subject_identity": [
      "A young woman, whose specific appearance and reddish-orange hair color are based on the reference image_19.png."
    ],
    "hair_style": [
      "Her reddish-orange hair is tied up into a messy, casual bun, similar to the style in image_19.png but less neat, with stray strands framing her face."
    ],
    "clothing": [
      "She is wearing a simple, light grey or faded blue t-shirt, similar in style to the one in image_22.png."
    ],
    "pose_and_action": [
      "She is sitting cross-legged on a bed, similar to the pose in image_19.png and image_22.png.",
      "She is holding a smartphone in front of her face with one hand, taking a mirror selfie, obscuring most of her face.",
      "Her other hand is resting on a crumpled white duvet."
    ],
    "environment_main": [
      "The setting is a dimly lit, bohemian-style bedroom, similar to the one in image_22.png.",
      "The room has a lived-in, cluttered, and cozy feel."
    ],
    "environment_furniture_and_objects": [
      "In the background, there is a vintage green-painted dresser with open drawers.",
      "On top of the dresser, there are various items like bottles, a small mirror, and personal objects.",
      "A white metal stool is visible near the dresser.",
      "A large mirror on the wall reflects the scene.",
      "A crumpled white duvet and blankets are on the bed."
    ],
    "lighting_details": [
      "The room is dimly lit with natural, soft light coming from a window (off-camera), creating a moody and intimate atmosphere, similar to the lighting in image_22.png.",
      "The lighting is not harsh but creates soft shadows."
    ],
    "Photography_style": [
      "A candid mirror selfie photograph.",
      "The photo has a film-like quality with visible grain, muted colors, and a slightly desaturated, warm tone, similar to the aesthetic of image.png."
    ]
  }
}
```

### 104. 带姿势和身份锁定的 2x2 拼贴提示

> 一个高度受限的 JSON 提示，用于生成 2x2 拼贴画，要求与上传的参考图像在面部识别、姿势、角度和构图上 100% 匹配，图像中是一位亚洲女性，身穿复古白色碎花连衣裙，头发上系着一个大大的蝴蝶结，置身于浪漫的复古室内环境中。

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "reference": {
      "face_identity": "uploaded reference image",
      "identity_lock": true,
      "pose_lock": true,
      "camera_angle_lock": true,
      "expression_lock": true,

      "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
      "pose_matching": "exactly match reference image poses, angles, framing, and body orientation",
      "no_variation_allowed": true
    },

    "panel_1": {
      "view": "front-facing portrait",
      "pose": "head slightly tilted, eyes toward camera, soft lips",
      "framing": "chest-up selfie angle",
      "expression": "calm, elegant",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_2": {
      "view": "back view",
      "pose": "standing facing mirror, arms raised slightly",
      "focus": "back of head and bow hairstyle",
      "framing": "upper-body rear shot",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_3": {
      "view": "mirror selfie",
      "pose": "phone covering part of face, body angled sideways",
      "framing": "waist-up",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_4": {
      "view": "side portrait",
      "pose": "head turned over shoulder looking into camera, holding bouquet close to chest",
      "expression": "soft romantic gaze",
      "framing": "upper torso",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "subject": {
      "gender": "female",
      "ethnicity": "Asian",
      "skin_tone": "fair with soft blush"
    },

    "hair": {
      "style": "long straight hair, half-up",
      "accessory": "{argument name=\"hair accessory\" default=\"large cream ribbon bow\"}",
      "placement": "exact position as reference image"
    },

    "outfit": {
      "dress": {
        "color": "white",
        "pattern": "{argument name=\"dress pattern\" default=\"blue floral print\"}",
        "style": "vintage puff-sleeve dress",

      },
      "jewelry": [
        "pearl necklace",
        "delicate gold pendant"
      ]
    },

    "environment": {

      ],
      "match_reference_background": true

      "shadow": "minimal",
      "match_reference": true

      "color_grading": "soft pastel"

### 106. 现代健身房里的全身镜自拍

**Author**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh)  **Date**: 2025-12-15  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的图像生成提示，用于创建一张高度逼真的年轻女性在现代健身房中拍摄的全身镜面自拍照，重点关注特定的服装、姿势和光照条件，同时保持参考图像中的身份锁定。

![现代健身房里的全身镜自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936176310_zyzf0k_G8N1UQsbEAAo6qG.jpg)

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "reference": {
      "face_identity": "use uploaded reference image",
      "identity_lock": true,
      "face_accuracy": "100% identical to reference — same facial structure, proportions, skin texture, expression, and details"
    },

    "subject": {
      "type": "young woman",
      "appearance": {
        "hair": {
          "color": "dark brown",
          "style": "long wavy hair with a half-up messy bun, loose strands framing the face"
        },
        "skin": {
          "tone": "same as reference image",
          "texture": "natural, realistic"
        },
        "expression": "calm, composed, slightly focused",
        "gaze": "looking at phone screen"
      },
      "pose": {
        "stance": "standing with one leg slightly forward",
        "hands": {
          "right": "holding a purple smartphone for a mirror selfie",
          "left": "holding a transparent water bottle with blue liquid"
        }
      }
    },

    "outfit": {
      "top": {
        "primary": "fitted short-sleeve white t-shirt",
        "layer": "white long-sleeve shirt tied around the waist"
      },
      "bottom": {
        "type": "high-waisted athletic leggings",
        "color": "navy blue"
      },
      "footwear": {
        "shoes": "white athletic sneakers",
        "socks": "white crew socks"
      }
    },

    "environment": {
      "location": "modern indoor gym",
      "features": [
        "large wall mirrors",
        "treadmills",
        "weight machines",
        "rubber gym flooring",
        "exercise mats on the floor"
      ],
      "reflection": "mirror seam visible vertically in frame"
    },

    "lighting": {
      "type": "bright overhead fluorescent gym lighting",
      "quality": "even, neutral illumination with minimal shadows"
    },

    "composition": {
      "shot_type": "full-body mirror selfie",
      "camera_angle": "eye-level",
      "framing": "centered subject",
      "style": "casual fitness lifestyle photograph"
    },

    "image_style": {
      "realism": "highly photorealistic",
      "detail": "sharp clothing textures and clear gym background",
      "mood": "clean, modern, casual",
      "resolution": "high resolution"
    }
  }

### 114. 带参考控制的复杂图像生成提示

**Author**: [AIossansan](https://x.com/toraaiuser2)  **Date**: 2025-12-14  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个针对 Nano Banana Pro 的高度结构化提示模板，指示模型忽略之前的图像，并严格使用两张参考图像来扮演特定角色：图像 A 用于角色设计（面部、发型、服装），图像 B 用于姿势和构图。它包含有关角色的详细说明和具体禁令。

![带参考控制的复杂图像生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991369525_21a0st_G8I_nUibYAESH6Y.jpg)
![带参考控制的复杂图像生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991369710_twxzx8_G8I_luNawAER7c4.jpg)
![带参考控制的复杂图像生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991370225_tm18em_G8I_6H7bMAA5iFe.jpg)
![带参考控制的复杂图像生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991374078_ht6s9g_G8JAAQUbsAEeT6U.jpg)

```
以前の画像や構図は一切参照しないでください（i2i禁止）。
以下のプロンプトに基づいて、ゼロから新しく描画してください。

【1. 参照画像の役割分担（重要）】* **画像A：** キャラクターデザイン（顔、髪型、服装）の参照元です。このデザインを**厳密に維持**してください。勝手なアレンジは禁止です。* **画像B：** ポーズと構図の参照元です。この骨組み通りのポーズをとらせてください。

【2. キャラクター詳細（画像Aと同一にする）】
（例：{argument name="キャラクター詳細" default="黒髪でロングヘアの少女。オフショルダーのサンタ服を着ている"}）

【3. アクション・構図（画像Bに従う）】
（例：{argument name="アクション構図" default="モデルのようなたたずまい。カメラ目線。海の浅瀬にたつ"}）

【4. 禁止事項】* キャラクターの髪色や服装を変更すること。* 指定した画像以外のポーズをとらせること。
```

[[Identity Preservation]] [[Character Design]] [[Prompt Engineering]] [[Pose Reference]]

```
Upscale the uploaded image to 4K resolution, preserving 100 % character consistency, original facial features, clothing details, and scene composition. Maintain original lighting, texture, and fine details such as hair strands, fabric texture, reflections, and shadows. Apply high-quality upscaling with sharp but natural edges, no distortions, and minimal AI artifacts. Keep the character’s identity, proportions, and expressions unchanged. Enhance clarity in skin texture, eyes, and background elements while preserving the original color palette and artistic style. Output a crisp, highly detailed, ultra-high-resolution image suitable for print and professional display.
```

### 122. 自信奢华的力量：身着黑色定制裤装的女性肖像

**Author**: Mansi Sanghani  **Date**: 2025-12-14  **Language**: en

> 此提示词可生成一张 4K、4:5 的照片级写实时尚编辑风格肖像，描绘一位特定女性主体。该女性主体的面部、发型、体型和肤色将严格匹配用户输入的参考图像，仅改变姿势、服装和环境。图像将她置于豪华宫殿或遗产酒店般的室内，自信地坐在雕花木椅上，身体略微前倾，身穿剪裁合体的黑色裤装，化着迷人的晚妆，高跟鞋清晰可见于抛光大理石地板上。图像采用温暖柔和的室内照明，景深为浅到中等，并辅以华丽、皇家风格的装饰元素（挂毯、带有深绿色花瓶的大理石基座），营造出优雅、强大的领导者/企业家美学，适合高端编辑或社交媒体使用。

        "subject seated prominently in the foreground",

        "high heels clearly visible with reflections or subtle shine on the floor"
      ],
      "clutter_level": "minimal, keep focus on the subject and key decor pieces"
    },
    "focus_and_depth_of_field": {

    },

    },

### 133. 超写实 3x3 网格肖像，身份固定

**Author**: [松果先森](https://x.com/songguoxiansen)  **Date**: 2025-12-14  **Language**: zh

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的复杂 JSON 格式提示词，用于生成一个人物的 3x3 网格拼贴画。该拼贴画将展示 9 种不同的表情、发型、服装和背景，同时严格保持所有面板中精确的面部身份和骨骼结构。这非常适合从单一参考图像创建一致的角色设定图或高质量、多样化的肖像。

![超写实 3x3 网格肖像，身份固定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936044685_z5rjob_G8Ge2crbAAAzXzS.jpg)

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "critical_instruction": "ABSOLUTE PRIORITY: Maintain identical facial structure across all panels. Do not alter underlying bone structure, nose shape, eye spacing, or jawline regardless of the expression being rendered. The identity must be unmistakable in every single shot.",
    "format": "3x3 grid collage",
    "subject": {
      "face_reference": "uploaded_photo",
      "face_identity_lock": "CRITICAL: fixed identity, zero deviation from reference facial features",
      "face_match_accuracy": "100% exact match enforced",
      "identity_preservation_details": "Ensure consistent interpupillary distance, exact nose bridge shape, and jaw structure in every panel.",
      "negative_constraints": [
        "do not morph nose shape",
        "do not change eye size or spacing",
        "do not alter cheekbone structure",
        "no plastic surgery look"
      ],
      "style": "hyper-realistic portrait photography, 8k resolution, raw photo aesthetic",
      "skin": "highly detailed natural skin texture, visible pores, subtle imperfections, realistic complexion, consistent across all lighting conditions",
      "camera_settings": "shot on Sony A7R IV, 85mm portrait lens, f/1.8 aperture, sharp focus on eyes, shallow depth of field"
    },

    "panels": [
      {
        "expression": "joyful",
        "pose": "bright natural smile (maintaining jaw structure), shoulders slightly raised",
        "hairstyle": "high ponytail with loose strands",
        "outfit": "pastel cotton hoodie",
        "background": "soft gradient sky blue studio backdrop"
      },
      {
        "expression": "surprised",
        "pose": "hands near face, wide eyes (without altering eye shape), natural reaction",
        "hairstyle": "loose natural wavy hair",
        "outfit": "casual cotton t-shirt",
        "background": "light peach studio backdrop"
      },
      {
        "expression": "sad",
        "pose": "head tilted down, emotional soft eyes",
        "hairstyle": "messy low bun",
        "outfit": "oversized wool sweater",
        "background": "muted lavender tone studio backdrop"
      },
      {
        "expression": "tender",
        "pose": "gentle smile, head slightly tilted",

        "outfit": "soft knit top",
        "background": "warm beige studio backdrop"

### 136. 角色“参与屏幕”揭示提示

**Author**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac)  **Date**: 2025-12-12  **Language**: ja

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的高度结构化、多层次的提示，旨在为基于参考图像的角色创建引人注目的“参战画面”或揭示闪屏图像。它严格保留了角色的身份和风格，同时将其置于 16:9 的构图中，并配有标题文本（“参战!!”）和一个简单的、富有氛围感的背景。

![角色“参与屏幕”揭示提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991058977_6lapjd_G8AaTaOagAIA6uY.jpg)
![角色“参与屏幕”揭示提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991058866_bgl41k_G8AaVdeagAQOaKo.jpg)
![角色“参与屏幕”揭示提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991059360_a7snc8_G8AaWfbagAELy_D.jpg)
![角色“参与屏幕”揭示提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991060920_zklgo4_G8AbixgawAA7MOt.jpg)

```
layering:
  order:
    - text_layer
    - character_layer
    - background_layer
  strict: true

subject:
  description: >
    Preserve the subject exactly as in the reference image, keeping all facial features,
    colors, hairstyle, clothing, and proportions. No redesign or reinterpretation.
  framing: >
    Bust-up composition (head to upper torso), making the subject appear large and prominent.
  integrity: full_identity_preservation
  detail_level: ultra_high_resolution
  micro_details: preserve_skin_texture_hair_edges_fabric_details

composition:
  aspect_ratio: "16:9"
  layout: >
    Subject positioned on one side; headline text on the opposite side.
  emphasis: >
    Strong presence on the character's upper body and expression.

action:
  description: >
    Minimal motion enhancement. Maintain the reference pose while adding subtle dramatic energy.

location:
  description: >
    Simple background created by interpreting the reference image’s mood.
    Use soft gradients, atmospheric glow, light particles, or abstract light rays.
    Avoid complex textures or any copyrighted shapes.
    Background must NOT contain any characters, silhouettes, faces, bodies,
    or blurred forms derived from the subject.
  background_feel: >
    Subtle, atmospheric, clean.
  allowed_elements: pure_color_gradients_light_abstract_shapes_only
  prohibit_subject_reuse_in_background: true

style:
  visual_style: >
    High-impact reveal-splash aesthetic with strong contrast between character and headline.
  text_effects: >
    Metallic, high-energy lettering with pronounced depth and perspective. No glow effects.
  character_rendering: >
    Extremely high-resolution rendering with sharp facial details, clean hair definition,
    precise edges, and crisp texture fidelity.
  background_style_rules: >
    Background must be purely non-figurative. No silhouettes, no blurred shapes,
    and no reused subject elements.
  ink_splash_rules: >
    Ink splash must be pure black only. No other colors, tinting, blending, or variation.

camera_lighting:
  camera_angle: from_reference
  lighting: >
    Enhance with dramatic key lighting and subtle rim highlights to emphasize the reveal.
  clarity: maximum_definition

colors:
  palette: >
    Background colors inferred from the reference image.
    Character name in metallic silver; announcement text in saturated yellow.
  mood: dramatic, heroic, high_energy

text:
  character_name: "{argument name="キャラクター名" default="キャラクター名"}"
  announcement_fixed: "参戦!!"
  placement: opposite_side_of_character
  p
```

[[Identity Preservation]]

### 141. 用于生成镜面自拍图像的详细 JSON 提示

**Author**: [Sienna](https://x.com/siennalovesai)  **Date**: 2025-12-12  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于 Gemini Nano Banana Pro，旨在生成一张年轻女性蹲姿照镜子自拍的超现实图像。该提示词包含面部保留、姿势、服装（祖母绿丝绸连衣裙）、环境（豪华酒店套房）、灯光以及具体的负面提示词等大量细节。

![用于生成镜面自拍图像的详细 JSON 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765990995237_swj0s5_G7-7V_CXMAADFe1.jpg)

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "face_preservation": {
      "use_reference_face": true,
      "accuracy": "match face exactly from reference image",
      "preserve_details": [
        "face shape",
        "eyebrows and eye structure",
        "natural makeup style",
        "lip shape and color",
        "hairline and hairstyle"
      ]
    },
    "subject": {
      "gender": "female",
      "description": "young woman taking a mirror selfie while squatting gracefully indoors",
      "pose": {
        "body_position": "squatting low with one knee forward, leaning slightly toward mirror",
        "head": "tilted slightly downward while looking at phone screen",
        "hands": [
          "right hand holding phone in front of face",
          "left hand resting on knee"
        ],
        "expression": "soft, calm expression"
      },
      "hair": {
        "style": "long dark brown hair in a half-up ponytail with a small clip",
        "texture": "smooth and straight"
      },
      "attire": {
        "dress": {
          "type": "emerald green silk maxi dress with spaghetti straps",
          "pattern": "plain with subtle drape",
          "details": "side slit exposing leg, low back design"

### 147. 门户场景生成提示

**Author**: [テツメモ｜AI図解×検証｜Newsletter](https://x.com/tetumemo)  **Date**: 2025-12-12  **Language**: ja

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细日式提示词，用于生成一个角色穿过发光椭圆形传送门的场景，将“现实世界”场景与“内部传送门”场景分隔开。它严格保持角色在参考图像中的原始风格（插画、动漫或照片），同时将内部传送门场景描绘成照片般真实且具有电影感的。角色被描绘成带着一丝悲伤的表情回望。

![门户场景生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991056617_pks4dh_G7-XmMeaQAAMxdT.jpg)

```
発光する楕円形のポータルが、{argument name="現実世界のシーン" default="伏見稲荷大社"} と {argument name="ポータル内のシーン" default="青いホログラムと屈折するネオンに照らされた、実写調・フォトリアルな未来都市のストリート。シネマティックな現実感を持つ。"} の間に存在している。

ポータルの外側には {argument name="現実世界のシーン" default="伏見稲荷大社"} が広がっており、リアルなテクスチャ、地に足のついた空気感、荒さや自然さを感じさせるトーンで描かれている。

ポータルの内側には {argument name="ポータル内のシーン" default="青いホログラムと屈折するネオンに照らされた、実写調・フォトリアルな未来都市のストリート。シネマティックな現実感を持つ。"} が存在し、完全にフォトリアルかつ実写調、シネマティックな表現で描かれている。  
ユーザーが添付した参照画像の種類に関係なく、ポータル内の世界は常に実写・現実的な表現を維持する。

{argument name="ポータル内のキャラクター" default="ユーザーが添付した画像を完全に基準とし、そのメディア特性・表現形式・質感を一切変更しない。"} はポータルを通り抜けながら、観る者の手をやさしく引いている。  
前へ進みつつも振り返り、少し物悲しそうな、控えめな表情でこちらを見つめている。  
その視線には、わずかな悲しさ、ためらい、言葉にできない感情が静かに表れている。

キャラクターの外見、画風、質感、レンダリング方式、メディア特性は、ユーザーが添付した画像のテイストを完全に保持すること。  
・参照画像がイラストの場合、キャラクターはイラスト表現のままとする  
・参照画像がアニメ調の場合、キャラクターはアニメ調のままとする  
・参照画像が写真の場合、キャラクターは写真表現（フォトリアル）のままとする  
いかなる場合でも、キャラクターの表現スタイルを他の表現形式へ変換してはならない。

ポータルは神秘的な青紫色の光を放っている。  
ポータルは二つの世界をつなぐ視覚的な境界として機能するが、キャラクター本来の表現テイストに影響を与えてはならない。  
光や縁の処理は、キャラクターの元の描画・撮影スタイルを尊重した形でなじませる。

任意の全体ビジュアルスタイル: {argument name="アートスタイル" default="添付画像由来のキャラクター表現と、実写世界との意図的なコントラスト。"}  

カメラアングル: 三人称視点。  
観る者の手が新しい世界へ引き込まれている様子が明確に見える構図。  
ブラーなし。  
キャラクターと環境は、それぞれの表現特性を保ったまま、シャープに描き分ける。  
アスペクト比: 2:3。
```

{

      "expression": "Subtle smile"
    },

      "accessories": "None"
    },

      "body_position": "Sits cross-legged on a bed",
      "interaction": "Laptop in front of her",
      "vibe": "Relaxed cozy pose"

> 一个高度精细、结构化的 JSON 提示，用于 Nano Banana Pro，详细描述了一张健身房镜子自拍。它指定了技术设置（8K，4:5 宽高比）、严格的面部保留，以及拍摄对象姿势（低蹲、手持手机）、服装（米黄色运动文胸、白色紧身裤）和健身房环境的微小细节，旨在生成高保真图像。

![粒状健身镜自拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765967746447_5b8py3_G76vS5mW8AAaugM.jpg)

```
{
  "project_settings": {
    "project_name": "Gym Mirror Selfie Series",
    "version": "4.0.0-granular",
    "target_model": "Stable Diffusion / Midjourney v6"
  },

      },

          "item": "Leggings pants",

### 174. 社论：夜间城市人像摄影中的身份保留

**Author**: [gemini_prompts](https://x.com/YeKyaHoRhaHaiBe)  **Date**: 2025-12-11  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张都市夜景中年轻女性的编辑级写实肖像，重点在于严格保留参考照片中的面部特征。它指定了复杂的灯光（暖色闪光灯、冷色阴影、轮廓光）、详细的服装（带文字的条纹针织毛衣），以及模拟胶片颗粒效果，以呈现高对比度、精致的画面。

![社论：夜间城市人像摄影中的身份保留](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765967722895_4ij8rp_G73jxYbbAAAKCs8.jpg)

```
"Young woman (make the face 100% identical to the photo I provided), fair skin, with a messy, loosely tied dark-brown hair bun a few strands falling naturally around the face for a soft, effortless look.
Pose (Updated):
She is seated, waist-up framing.
Body slightly turned to the left; posture relaxed and natural.
Right hand resting casually on her lap or lightly touching the side of the chair.
Left hand holding the strap of the shoulder bag, which rests against her torso.
Head facing the camera; eyes looking softly into the lens.
Expression calm, slightly aloof, with a subtle closed-mouth smile - editorial, understated mood.
Clothing & Accessories:
Thick horizontal striped knit sweater ({argument name="sweater color 1" default="pink"}, {argument name="sweater color 2" default="mustard yellow"}, {argument name="sweater color 3" default="purple"}, {argument name="sweater color 4" default="white"}), slightly oversized with distressed collar and hem edges.
Large chest typography: "{argument name="typography text" default="DEADLY DOLL"}"
Black leather belt with simple buckle.
Dark leather shoulder bag (strap visible). Chunky silver rings on right hand; smaller rings on left hand.
Minimal natural makeup (matte skin, soft lip sheen).
Background & Atmosphere:
Nighttime urban street scene viewed behind her: blurred vehicle lights, traffic signals, neon accents.
Motion blur + bokeh, giving a lively city feel while she remains isolated by light.
Warm highlights on her face, cooler-toned shadows around her seat.
Lighting:
Main warm flash (around 3200K) slightly above eye level. Soft fill light from the right to keep sweater texture clear.
Subtle rim/backlight to separate her messy bun and shoulders from the dark background.
Fine 35mm film grain for analog realism.
Composition:
Portrait orientation, medium close-up (waist-up).
Face placed slightly left of center (rule of thirds).
Shallow depth of field (f/2.2-f/3.5): sharp on face and sweater, background softly blurred. Camera angle: eye-level or slightly high for a refined editorial feel.
Technical Notes:
35mm or 50mm prime (f/1.8-f/2.8).
Shutter: 1/125-1/200.
ISO 400-1600 for film grain or ISO 100 for flash-sharp clarity.
Output: 4K/6000x4000 px, 300 dpi.
Keep natural skin texture, sweater knit details, and metallic ring reflections.
Color & Post-Processing:
Warm midtones, teal-leaning shadows, medium-high contrast. Slightly boosted sweater saturation; natural skin tones.
Soft vignette around edges to keep focus on face.
Fine analog-style grain applied evenly.
Negative Prompt:
avoid cartoon, anime, extra limbs, distorted hands, unnatural skin smoothing, HDR look, blown highlights, watermark, low resolution, oversaturation, excessive lens flare."
```

### 178. 电影级航空母舰飞行员肖像（身份锁定）

**Author**: [Javeriya Editor](https://x.com/JadoonKhan281)  **Date**: 2025-12-10  **Language**: en

> 一个高度具体、电影化的 Gemini Nano Banana 3.0 Pro 提示词，要求绝对保留女性模特的身份特征。场景设定在航空母舰驾驶舱内，背景是浩瀚的海洋。提示词详细描述了模特的醒目着装（白色露脐挂脖上衣、黑色颈圈）、粉色头发、动漫风格妆容，并使用了精确的摄影参数（85mm 镜头、f/1.4 光圈、8K 分辨率），以实现超现实、冒险的美学效果。

![电影级航空母舰飞行员肖像（身份锁定）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509777224_anklyp_G70JES0bAAAD0AF.jpg)

```
Ultra-realistic 8K portrait of a female model in her twenties, identity preservation is ABSOLUTE with 100% facial and body alignment. The model is seated in the cockpit of an aircraft carrier, high above the vast, deep blue ocean. The backdrop features expansive sky with a soft gradient of clouds, the endless ocean stretching out behind her. The model wears a glossy white halter crop top, black faux leather choker with a metallic lock, matching black cuffs on her wrists, and a glossy black pilot-style cap with a metallic winged heart emblem. The wind is softly blowing, creating gentle movement in her long, voluminous pink hair.

Mood and Concept: Bold, cinematic, and adventurous with a hint of rebellious energy. The setting evokes a sense of power, freedom, and adrenaline. Her posture is strong and confident, seated comfortably in the cockpit, with one hand resting on the armrest and the other on her lap, showcasing the sleekness of the outfit and accessories. The ocean breeze subtly lifts her hair, adding a sense of movement and life to the scene.

Outfit and Styling:
Glossy white halter crop top, tight fit, accentuating her toned midriff.
Black faux leather choker-style collar with a subtle silver lock at the front.
Matching black cuffs on both wrists with a polished, reflective finish.
Glossy black cap with a shiny metallic winged heart emblem on the front.

Hair and Makeup:
Hair: Soft, voluminous pink hair in long, tousled waves, subtly lifted by the sea breeze. The hair has a glossy sheen, with some strands gently flowing, adding a sense of realism and movement.

Makeup: Bold, anime-inspired makeup with dramatic eyeliner and large, doe-like eyes. The eyebrows are defined with a strong arch. Her lips are painted in a soft, glossy pink MLBB shade to complement her vibrant hair color, giving her an ethereal, almost otherworldly vibe. Skin has a porcelain, flawless finish.

Photography Specs:
Canon EOS R5 with 85mm f1.2 lens.
Aperture f1.4 for a shallow depth of field and soft bokeh background.
Shutter speed 1/250 s.
ISO 200 for perfect exposure in daylight with the soft sea breeze lighting.
Aspect Ratio 5:7

Detail and Finish:
Soft rim light tracing her face and highlighting the contours of her features, with a soft glow from the sunlight filtering through the cockpit.
Glossy reflections from her cap, top, and accessories for a tactile, photorealistic finish.
The movement of the hair adds dynamic realism, with the breeze from the open cockpit slightly blowing it back and away from her face.

Negative Prompt: Do not render any cartoonish, anime, or stylized features. Avoid exaggerated proportions, flat shading, or unrealistic textures. Ensure the image remains photorealistic with natural human proportions, true-to-life lighting, and realistic textures.
```

### 179. 新黑色都市夜景人像，带面部保留

**Author**: [Ditherly - Creative AI Hub](https://x.com/ditherly_art)  **Date**: 2025-12-10  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张在霓虹灯照耀的城市小巷中，情绪化、电影感的肖像。它要求精确保留参考图像中人物的面部和发型，描绘他们身穿街头风格服装，在刺眼的顶灯下蹲伏，并带有强烈的光晕和模拟胶片颗粒效果。

![新黑色都市夜景人像，带面部保留](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509704071_wanxl0_G7WmZcTW4AA8jZF.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation": {
    "identity_requirements": {
      "face": {
        "preserve_original": true,
        "exact_match": true,
        "description": "Precisely maintain the subject’s original facial structure, proportions, and recognizable identity from the reference image."
      },
      "hair": {
        "preserve_original": true,
        "exact_match": true,
        "description": "Reproduce the subject’s hairstyle exactly as seen in the reference image — same length, parting, texture, and flow."
      }
    },

    "setting": {
      "location": "gritty neon-lit urban alleyway",
      "background": {
        "elements": [
          "harsh overhead alley light",

### 184. 超广角动态姿势重制提示词

**Author**: [xiaobeiLin](https://x.com/linxiaobei888)  **Date**: 2025-12-07  **Language**: zh

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的综合性中文提示，专注于编辑现有图像，以创建一张戏剧性的、超现实的、超广角照片。它要求严格保留身份和位置，同时允许完全改变拍摄角度、透视（仰视、俯视、倾斜角）和动态姿势，以强调透视缩短效果。

![超广角动态姿势重制提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991063523_5aptn0_G7jKx80aYAAwtja.jpg)
![超广角动态姿势重制提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991064165_scbewl_G7jKx8xacAAzN4p.jpg)
![超广角动态姿势重制提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991064057_ilbqwq_G7jKx9ma8AAsMiO.jpg)
![超广角动态姿势重制提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991065599_wrb52k_G7jKx8zbsAAQDVq.jpg)

```
极广角透视与动态姿势重制编辑
这是对原始图像的编辑，而非生成新角色。
请将原始图像作为严格参考，用于确定：
 * 人物的身份、发型和整体时尚风格，
 * 背景和地点的总体类型（相同的街道、相同的房间、相同的海滩、相同的建筑风格等）。
允许完全改变相机位置、角度和姿势，但必须保持场景在同一地点，并保留同一人物和服装设计。
相机与透视：
 * 使用超广角或鱼眼感镜头（约 12–18mm 全画幅外观）。
 * 相机角度必须与原图有显著变化：使用戏剧性的角度，例如：
   * 从正下方向上看的仰视（虫视），
   * 从正上方并向下看的俯视（鸟视），
   * 极贴近地面的低角度，
   * 从上方拍摄的高角度，
   * 倾斜的荷兰角（Dutch angles）。
 * 始终创造强烈的**透视缩短（foreshortening）**效果：靠近镜头的身体部位看起来巨大，而身体其余部分在透视中远去。
 * 最终结果必须看起来像是一张大胆的时尚或街头照片，完全写实，而非插画或动漫。
背景一致性：
 * 保持与原图相同的地点：相同的街道、桥梁、房间、工作室、海滩以及相同的总体结构和材质。
 * 不要将背景替换为完全不同的地方。
 * 由于相机角度发生变化，看到环境的不同部分是允许且预期的。
 * 当新区域出现时，请逻辑地扩展原始环境（相同的建筑、栅栏、路标、墙壁、颜色、材料、光照风格），就像相机在同一个地方移动一样。
靠近镜头的身体部位（1–2 个部位，有时 3 个）：
 * 在每次编辑中，选择一到两个主要身体部位极度靠近镜头（在更复杂的姿势中有时甚至可以是三个）。
 * 在不同图像间进行变化，不要总是使用相同的身体部位。
 * 允许靠近镜头的部位包括：
   * 一只或双手/手指伸向相机，
   * 一只或双脚/鞋/靴子靠近镜头，
   * 膝盖或大腿，
   * 脸部非常靠近镜头，
   * 倾斜姿势下的肩膀或胸部靠近镜头。
 * 选定的身体部位应极度靠近镜头，几乎接触到它，并具有可见的皮肤纹理、织物纹理和逼真的广角畸变。
姿势与整体身姿（复杂且多变）：
 * 创造强烈、酷炫、动态的姿势，以匹配极端的透视。
 * 随机使用不同类型的姿势，包括：
   * 站立并伸出一条腿或一只手朝向相机，
   * 蹲伏或蹲低在地面，
   * 坐在地板或物体上，
   * 躺在地上，腿或脚朝向镜头，
   * 咄咄逼人地向相机前倾，
   * 扭转身体、交叉双腿或拱起背部以形成更动态的线条。
 * 允许复杂的姿势，例如：
   * 双手在镜头附近做出形状（剪刀手、三角形、相框、指向观众），
   * 双脚朝向镜头，
   * 一只手和一只脚都在前景变大，
   * 脸部靠近镜头，同时手或脚也在透视中可见。
 * 即使有极端的透视缩短，也要保持可信的解剖结构。
角度与态度（随机化）：
 * 随机化相机角度和方向（上、下、侧面、荷兰式倾斜），同时保持构图视觉平衡且有力。
 * 保持酷炫、自信和时尚/编辑或街头风格的氛围，具体取决于原始服装。
 * 面部表情可以变化（严肃、顽皮、自信、神秘），但必须看起来仍是同一个人。
光照与渲染：
 * 保持与原作相似的总体时间段和光照氛围（白天与夜晚，室内与室外，软光与硬光），但可以增强对比度和色彩，使图像有力且具有戏剧性。
 * 保持逼真的阴影和与地面或地板的接触点。
 * 高分辨率，清晰的细节，具有清晰的皮肤纹理、织物编织和材质高光。
变化与随机性：
 * 每次编辑应看起来与原图和其他编辑明显不同，具有不同的：
   * 相机角度，
   * 姿势类型，
   * 最靠近镜头的身体部位，
   * 方向（直、倾斜、从上方、从下方）。
 * 避免重复完全相同的“单脚特写”构图；产生各种动态姿势和角度。
严格规则：
 * 不要把人变成别人。
 * 不要改变服装类型；只能通过姿势、透视和衣物的微小自然运动来重新造型。
 * 不要将场景移动到完全不同的位置；始终停留在原始地点的合理延伸范围内。
 * 不要添加文本、徽标、水印或平面设计元素。
 * 不要切换到绘画、插图或动漫风格；保持写实。
总结：
将原始照片转变为一张具有极端相机角度（包括从正下方或正上方观看）的戏剧性、写实、超广角照片，其中一个或多个身体部位紧贴镜头并显得巨大，身体其余部分在透视中后退，同一人物在原始环境的一致扩展版本中摆出时尚、复杂、有力的姿势。
```

[[Identity Preservation]] [[Image Editing]] [[Dynamic Pose]] [[Perspective Distortion]]

### 186. 情侣 MacBook 屏幕自拍模拟提示词

**Author**: [Mehal Kumar](https://x.com/Mehal_Kay)  **Date**: 2025-12-03  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的 JSON 配置，用于模拟一个超逼真的 MacBook 屏幕，其中显示一对特定情侣的 Photo Booth 自拍照，包括物理屏幕伪影、UI 布局和严格的身份保留设置。

![情侣 MacBook 屏幕自拍模拟提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909300815_o2w1ud_G7QjKGEbEAAR6Ig.jpg)

```
{
  "task_configuration": {
    "task_type": "screen_simulation_photorealism",
    "target_model": "SDXL_1.0_Refiner",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
    "resolution": {
      "width": 1152,
      "height": 1536
    }
  },
  "visual_hierarchy": {
    "layer_1_physical_macro": {
      "camera_angle": "Downward-angled, high-angle",
      "framing": "MacBook screen filling 95% of frame",
      "surface_imperfections": [
        "subtle pixel-grid texture (moire)",
        "tiny dust particles on glass",
        "faint ambient light reflection on glossy screen",
        "fingerprint smudges"
      ],
      "foreground_anchor": "Thin strip of physical keyboard visible at lower edge"
    },
    "layer_2_digital_interface": {
      "theme": "Dark Mode (macOS)",
      "window_layout": {
        "left_panel": "Spotify 'Liked Songs' playlist (dimmed)",
        "right_panel": "Photo Booth live-preview window (dominant focus)"
      }
    },
    "layer_3_nested_subject_content": {
      "context": "Inside the Photo Booth window",
      "environment": "Dim bedroom, off-white wall, rumpled bedding",
      "lighting_simulation": "Cool screen glow mixed with warm skin tones, deep nocturnal shadows",
      "subjects": {
        "shared_attributes": [
          "Oversized black hoodies",
          "Hoods pushed back (faces fully visible)",
          "Reclining pose",
          "Looking at screen"
        ],
        "subject_a_guy": {
          "identity_target": "{argument name="guy reference image" default="2nd image attached"}",
          "action": "Holding phone in right hand with clear reflective case",
          "position": "Right/Center"
        },
        "subject_b_girl": {
          "identity_target": "{argument name="girl reference image" default="1st image attached"}",
          "action": "Resting closely beside Subject A",
          "position": "Left/Center"
        }
      }
    }
  },
  "prompt_assembly": {
    "positive_prompt": "Hyper-realistic downward shot of a MacBook screen. The screen surface has visible dust, pixel grid, and reflection. The screen displays a Photo Booth window showing a couple in a dark room. [Subject Descriptions]. They are wearing black hoodies. The lighting is low-key, candid, nocturnal, blue-ish screen glow. High fidelity, raw photo, unedited.",
    "negative_prompt": "vector art, screenshot, flat digital image, clean glass, perfect screen, daylight, bright studio lights, cartoon, 3d render, painting, watermark"
  },
  "identity_preservation_settings": {
    "strictness_level": "CRITICAL",
    "methodology": {
      "face_restoration": false,
      "note": "Disable generic face restorers (CodeFormer) to avoid 'plastic' look. Use IP-Adapter.",
      "control_net_stack_multiline_placeholder": "[ControlNet configuration continues here]"
    }
  }
}
```

[[Identity Preservation]] [[Couple Portrait]]

### 192. 高保真换脸任务定义

**Author**: [Spicy Success](https://x.com/spicyysuccess)  **Date**: 2026-02-21  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 定义高保真换脸任务的结构化 JSON 提示。指令强调无缝、超真实的融合，保留源身份，匹配肤色和表情，并保持原始背景和构图细节。

![高保真换脸任务定义](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771741695019_yhyyta_HBrFTtgbgAE6U4A.jpg)
![高保真换脸任务定义](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771741695023_ngmk6p_HBrFTtLbgAA_kwv.jpg)

```
"task": "face_swap",
  "model": "nano_banana_pro",
  "instructions": {
    "primary_goal": "Transfer the face from source image (image1) onto the subject in target image (image2) with seamless, ultra-realistic integration",
    "source_mapping": {
      "face_source": "image1",
      "face_target": "image2",
      "preserve_source_identity": true
    },
    "identity": {
      "match_skin_tone": true,
      "match_facial_expression": true,
      "maintain_face_structure": true
    },
    "blending": {
      "seamless_edges": true,
      "match_lighting": true,
      "match_color_grading": true,
      "preserve_shadows_highlights": true,
      "no_visible_artifacts": true
    },
    "background": {
      "preserve_original_background": true,
      "preserve_environment_details": true,
      "no_changes_to_objects": true,
      "no_blur_or_distortion": true
    },
    "composition": {
      "keep_original_pose": true,
      "keep_camera_angle": true,
      "keep_framing": true,
      "maintain_depth_of_field": true
    },
    "quality": {
      "ultra_realistic": true,
      "high_resolution": true,
      "natural_texture": true,
      "no_ai_look": true
```

### 197. 使用 Tiny Workers 进行图像到图像的转换

**Author**: [Sharon Riley](https://x.com/Just_sharon7)  **Date**: 2026-01-31  **Language**: en

> 一个用于图像到图像转换的结构化 JSON 提示，指示模型在添加微小的人类工人执行特定动作（如清扫颜料或滚动油漆）时，保留原始图像的背景和颜色，并保持缓慢、自然的运动风格。

![使用 Tiny Workers 进行图像到图像的转换](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927661665_ps3l7i_G__szH7bEAMUG0H.jpg)

```
{
  "base_image": "use_uploaded_image_exactly_as_is",
  "instructions": {
    "preserve": {
      "background": true,
      "colors": true,
      "shadows": true,
      "water": true,
      "sand": true,
      "palette": true
    },
    "subjects": [
      {
        "type": "tiny_human_worker",
        "actions": [
          {"action": "sweep", "target": "pigment"},
          {"action": "roll_paint", "target": "color_blocks"},
          {"action": "climb", "target": "ladder", "careful": true},
          {"action": "carry", "object": "small_bucket", "place_down": true},
          {"action": "fix_edge", "tool": "brush", "target": "color_block"}
        ],
        "movement_style": "small_natural_slow"
      }
    ],
    "effects": {
      "special_effects": false,
      "light_effects": false,
      "glow": false,
      "smoke": false
    },
    "camera": {
      "movement": false
    },
    "objects": {
      "add": false
    },
    "text": {
      "add": false
    },
    "sound": false
  }
}
```

### 198. 图片编辑提示：徽标集成

**Author**: [underwood](https://x.com/underwoodxie96)  **Date**: 2026-01-31  **Language**: en

> Nano Banana Pro 指令提示：
> 
> 请将此 logo 整合到现有图像中。
> 
> **主体姿势调整：**
> * 将头部转向左侧。
> * 露出微笑。
> * 用左手指向 logo。
> 
> **Logo 放置：**
> * 让 logo 漂浮在主体上半身的正上方。
> * 确保 logo 保持其原始背景。

![图片编辑提示：徽标集成](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927691273_ul5x81_G_9ftnoakAAPCkn.jpg)

```
keep the girl’s character and pose from Image 2; have her turn her head toward the camera and smile; raise her left hand, make a fist, and point toward the logo from Image 1.  The logo should float above her upper body, fully visible with its original background color preserved.  No UI overlays.
```
